			\draw[ellC=560, rotate around={-133.5445:(64*\xStep,1*\yStep)}] (64*\xStep,1*\yStep) ellipse (6.288 and 1.044);
			\draw[ellC=560, rotate around={-43.5445:(64*\xStep,0*\yStep)}] (64*\xStep,0*\yStep) ellipse (1.044 and 6.288);
		\end{axis}
	\end{tikzpicture}
\end{document}
